English

The implication is that there is no answer to this question
except that it was the Lord’s will to do so.
Therefore why should we perform or adopt any up─Бya (for securing His protection)?

Some say, therefore, that, of His own accord,
and at the time when He chooses, the Lord saves us
and that the Lord bestows His grace on His servants
and protects them
when He is pleased to do so
and that no endeavour of any kind is incumbent on us.

Espa├▒ol

La implicaci├│n es que no hay respuesta a esta pregunta.
Excepto que era la voluntad del Se├▒or hacerlo.
Por lo tanto, ┬┐por qu├й deber├нamos realizar o adoptar cualquier up─Бya (para asegurar su protecci├│n)?

Algunos dicen, por lo tanto, que, por su propia cuenta,
y en el momento en que elige, el Se├▒or nos salva
y que el Se├▒or otorga su gracia a sus siervos
y los protege
Cuando se complace en hacerlo
y que no nos corresponde ning├║n esfuerzo de ning├║n tipo.

English

This doubt may be cleared as follows :-
Although I┼Ыvara is omnipotent,
He makes the man adopt some gesture, some means (vy─Бja) or pretext on his part
and, in consideration of it, protects him
in order that the faults of partiality and cruelty (vaiс╣гamya, n─Бirghс╣Ыс╣Зya) may not stain Him.

Espa├▒ol

Esta duda puede ser despejada de la siguiente manera:-

Aunque I┼Ыvara es omnipotente, Hace que el hombre adopte alg├║n gesto, de alguna manera (vy─Бja) o pretexto de su parte
y, en consideraci├│n, lo protege
Para que las fallas de la parcialidad y la crueldad (Vaiс╣гamya, N─Бirghс╣Ыс╣Зya) no lo manchen.

English

The Alwar himself has declared this truth in :-

“I said “Tirumalirunjolai”
and immediately, the Lord of Lakс╣гm─л
filled my mind with His presence.”

(The Vy─Бja, endeavour, or gesture, here,
is the utterance of the word Tirumalirunjolai by the Alwar).

Espa├▒ol

El propio Alwar ha declarado esta verdad en:-

“Dije “Tirumalirunjolai”
E inmediatamente, el Se├▒or de Lakс╣гm─л
llen├│ mi mente con su presencia “.

(El Vy─Бja, el esfuerzo o el gesto, aqu├н,
es la expresi├│n de la palabra tirumalirunjolai por el Alwar).

рдИрд╢реНрд╡рд░рд╕реНрдп рдХрд░реНрдорд╛рдиреБрд░реВрдк-рдлрд▓-рдкреНрд░рджрддреНрд╡рд╛-рднрд╛рд╡реЗ

рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдореН рдЕрд╕реНрдпрд╛рд╡рд╕рд░реЛ рди рдЬрд╛рдд

рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдПрддрддреН рдХрд╛рд░реНрдп-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖-рджрд░реНрд╢рдирд╛рддреН рдХрд▓реНрдкрд┐рддрдореН ред

English

and I┼Ыvara has to bestow, on each individual, the rewards or punishments
that are in accordance with such karma.

If He were to do otherwise,
He would be tainted with partiality (and injustice).

I┼Ыvara did not make the person adopt the vy─Бja before,
as the time for the ripening of the fruit of the karma had not yet come.

Therefore, from the effect we have to infer the cause, as stated above.

Espa├▒ol

y i┼Ыvara tiene que otorgar, en cada individuo, las recompensas o castigos
que est├бn de acuerdo con tal karma.

Si fuera a hacer lo contrario,
Estar├нa contaminado con la parcialidad (e injusticia).

I┼Ыvara no hizo que la persona adoptara el Vy─Бja antes,
Como el momento de la maduraci├│n del fruto del karma a├║n no hab├нa llegado.

Por lo tanto, por el efecto tenemos que inferir la causa, como se indic├│ anteriormente.

English

The subsidiary cause (sahak─Бri k─Бraс╣Зa ) is the vy─Бja (bhakti or prapatti)
which extinguishes the Lord’s punishment (hitherto) acting as a hindrance or obstacle.
Bhakti and prapatti
which are adopted as vy─Бja to secure I┼Ыvara’s favour,
are, themselves, the result of His compassion
due to special acts of merit.

These reveal I┼Ыvara’s omnipotent and compassionate nature.

Espa├▒ol

La causa subsidiaria (Sahak─Бri k─Бraс╣Зa) es el Vy─Бja (Bhakti o Prapatti)
que extingue el castigo del Se├▒or (hasta ahora) actuando como un obst├бculo.
Bhakti y Prapatti
que se adoptan como Vy─Бja
para asegurar el favor de I┼Ыvara,
son, ellos mismos, el resultado de su compasi├│n

English

But the compassion of a person
who is also omnipotent
can accomplish whatever is desired
and will bring delight to him
and be the cause of immediately relieving the distress of those who seek his help
and of giving them what they long for.

Espa├▒ol

Pero la compasi├│n de una persona
quien tambi├йn es omnipotente
puede lograr lo que se desee
y le traer├б deleite
y ser la causa de aliviar inmediatamente la angustia de aquellos que buscan su ayuda
y de darles lo que anhelan.

English

In regard to incarnations, it has been said,

“In the distresses of men,
┼Ъr─л R─Бma is greatly distressed”.

(It may be asked how this distress can be reconciled
with the delight spoken of above).

It means only this:
that this distress is only in order to
give delight to those who are worthy of His grace.
In the case of wicked men with the nature of Asuras,
the distress assumed by the avat─Бr
is to make the evil-doer become deluded into thinking
that he is not I┼Ыvara’s incarnation.

Espa├▒ol

Con respecto a las encarnaciones, se ha dicho,

“En las angustias de los hombres,
┼Ъr─л R─Бma est├б muy angustiado “.

(Se le puede preguntar c├│mo se puede reconciliar esta angustia
con el deleite mencionado de arriba).

Significa solo esto:
que esta angustia es solo para
Dar deleite a los que son dignos de su gracia.

En el caso de los hombres malvados con la naturaleza de Asuras,
la angustia asumida por el avat─Бr
es hacer que el malhechor se enga├▒e a pensar
que ├йl no es la encarnaci├│n de I┼Ыvara.

English

That is why it is said,

“The Upaniс╣гads state that
the Lord of ┼Ъr─л creates, maintains, controls and does such other things
in regard to sentient and non-sentient things,
only for His own sake.
It is therefore, O, Lord of ┼Ъr─лraс╣Еga,
Thy nature to be the means of salvation (up─Бya ) for the j─лva
and also the object of attainment.
Therefore I seek Thee as my up─Бya without any thought of my own interests.”

Espa├▒ol

Por eso se dice

“Los Upaniс╣гads indican que

Tu naturaleza es el medio de salvaci├│n (up─Бya) para el j─лva
y tambi├йn el objeto de logro.
Por lo tanto, te busco como mi up─Бya
sin pensar en mis propios intereses “.

Since Bhagav─Бn is the seat of the activity for the good of others,
He is the Saviour of those who seek refuge under Him
and since He places Himself in the place of other up─Бyas (like par─Бbhakti) (in order to protect them),
He is also the up─Бya.

English

(2) The injunction to perform prapatti is contained in the words,

“Seek refuge under me alone”.

Some say that
it is not an injunction to perform prapatti
and that this prapatti should be considered as an attribute of the person specified.

We answer as follows :–
This attribute cannot be held as that of the person so concerned or qualified,
as it does not satisfy the definition of an adjectival attribute.

(“He who desires svarga should perform the Jyotiс╣гс╣нoma sacrifice”.
Here, who desires svarga is an attribute or adjective of the person
and the injunction is that he should perform the sacrifice.
In Mam Ekam Saranam Vraja,
the prapatti has to be performed after hearing the vidhi or injunction;
it did not exist before, like the desire for svarga in the example cited.
Therefore, it is not an attribute;
besides vraja is a verb that prescribes an action.)

This statement is therefore contrary to pram├вna or authority.

Espa├▒ol

(2) El mandato para realizar Prapatti
est├б contenido en las palabras,

“Busque refugio bajo m├н solo”.

Algunos dicen que
No es una orden para realizar Prapatti
y que este Prapatti debe considerarse
como un atributo de la persona especificada.

Respondemos de la siguiente manera:-
Este atributo no puede mantenerse
como el de la persona tan preocupada o calificada,
ya que no satisface la definici├│n de un atributo adjetivo .

(“El que desea que Svarga deber├нa realizar el sacrificio de Jyotiс╣гс╣нoma”.
Aqu├н, qui├йn desea svarga es un atributo o adjetivo de la persona
Y la orden es que debe realizar el sacrificio.
En “Mam Ekam Saranam Vraja”,
El Prapatti debe realizarse despu├йs de escuchar el Vidhi o orden;
No exist├нa antes, como el deseo de Svarga en el ejemplo citado.
Por lo tanto, no es un atributo;
Adem├бs, Vraja es un verbo que prescribe una acci├│n.)

Por lo tanto, esta declaraci├│n es contraria a Pram├вna o autoridad.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рддрд╕реНрдп рдкреНрд░рд╛рдзрд╛рдиреНрдпрдВ рдЪ
рдкреНрд░рд╕рд╛рджрдиреИрдГ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдмрдиреНрдзрдХреЗ рдирд┐рдЧреНрд░рд╣реЗ рд╢рд╛рдиреНрддреЗ рд╕рддрд┐
рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рднрд╛рд╡рд┐рдХрд╛рдиреБрднрд╡рд╕реНрдп рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЬрдХрддреНрд╡рд╛рддреН ред

English

Siddhop─Бya is of prime importance, because
if, by proper propitiation, the punishment of the Lord is cancelled,
it becomes helpful for the enjoyment or experience (of Bhagav─Бn)
which is natural to the Self (in its purity).

Espa├▒ol

Siddhop─Бya es de gran importancia, porque
Si, por propiciaci├│n adecuada, el castigo del Se├▒or se cancela,
se vuelve ├║til para el disfrute o la experiencia (de Bhagav─Бn)
que es natural para el yo (en su pureza).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

[[резрепрем]]

рддрддреН рдХрдердореН рдЗрддрд┐ рдЪреЗрддреН—
рд░рддреНрдирд╕реНрдп рдорд╛рд▓рд┐рдиреНрдпреЗ рдирд╖реНрдЯреЗ рд╕рддрд┐
рдЬрд╛рдпрдорд╛рдирдГ рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рднрд╛рд╡рд┐рдХрдГ рдкреНрд░рднрд╛-рд╡рд┐рдХрд╛рд╕реЛ
рдпрдерд╛ рддрджреН-рдЕрдиреБрд░реВрдк рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рд╕рдВрдХрд▓реНрдк-рдорд╛рддреНрд░-рдирд┐рдмрдиреНрдзрдиреЛ рднрд╡рддрд┐,
рддрдерд╛ рдореБрдХреНрддрд╕реНрдп рдЬрд╛рдпрдорд╛рдирд╛ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди-рд╡рд┐рдХрд╛рд╕рд╛рджрдпреЛрд╜рдкрд┐
рддрджреН-рдЕрдиреБрд░реВрдк-рд╡реНрдпрд╡рд╕реНрдерд┐рдд-рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рд╕рдВрдХрд▓реНрдк-рдирд┐рдмрдиреНрдзрдирд╛ рднрд╡рдиреНрддрд┐ ред

English

If it is asked how this happens, the answer is as follows:–
When the gem is cleansed of the dust (enveloping it),
it shines with a natural radiance,
but this natural radiance is due only to the will of I┼Ыvara
that ordains its having radiance.
So also the expansion of knowledge and other attributes which the mukta acquires
are due to the will of I┼Ыvara, which ordains them.

Espa├▒ol

Si se pregunta c├│mo sucede esto, la respuesta es la siguiente:-
Cuando la gema se limpia del polvo (envuelto),
brilla con un resplandor natural,
Pero este resplandor natural se debe solo a la voluntad de I┼Ыvara
que ordena que tenga un resplandor.
As├н tambi├йn la expansi├│n del conocimiento y otros atributos que el Mukta adquiere
se deben a la voluntad de I┼Ыvara, que les ordena.

Learned men expressed this idea briefly in the ┼Ыloka :

“All things have their being in accordance with Thy will;
among them some are ever pleasing to Thee;
they are eternal;
Thy noble attributes which are, by nature, subject to Thee
illustrate this truth to us”.

“Todas las cosas tienen su estar de acuerdo con tu voluntad;
Entre ellos, algunos son siempre agradables para ti; son eternos;
Tus nobles atributos que, por naturaleza, est├бn sujetos a ti
Ilustrar esta verdad para nosotros “.

English

The ┼Ыloka which says:

“The Lord who took the necessary means or up─Бya for making me live,
while yet in my mother’s womb -
is He now asleep or is He now dead
in regard to the means to be adopted
for making me live after being born ?”

- this is sometimes quoted in support of the statement that the Lord is alone the up─Бya
and that the j─лva has to do nothing at all by way of up─Бya or vy─Бja.
It should be taken only as meaning that we should not seek any other protector
(and not to forbid man from any form of endeavour).

Espa├▒ol

El ┼Ъloka que dice:

“El Se├▒or que tom├│ los medios necesarios o up─Бya por hacerme vivir,
Mientras a├║n en el vientre de mi madre -
┬┐Est├б ahora dormido o ahora est├б muerto?
con respecto a los medios a adoptar
Por hacerme vivir despu├йs de haber nacido? "

- Esto a veces se cita en apoyo de la declaraci├│n de que el Se├▒or est├б solo el up─Бya
y que el J─лva no tiene que hacer nada en absoluto a trav├йs de Up─Бya o Vy─Бja.
Debe tomarse solo como significado que no debemos buscar ning├║n otro protector
(y no prohibir al hombre de ninguna forma de esfuerzo).
